Introduction

Base URL: https://api.dev.jumpintojob.com

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Authenticating requests

This API is not authenticated.

Endpoints

fields required: email, password, remember_me

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "https://api.dev.jumpintojob.com/api/v1/auth/user/login" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"email\": \"davis.leone@example.com\",
    \"password\": \"V<{$k,\",
    \"remember_me\": true
}"

const url = new URL(
    "https://api.dev.jumpintojob.com/api/v1/auth/user/login"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "email": "davis.leone@example.com",
    "password": "V<{$k,",
    "remember_me": true
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (401):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
x-ratelimit-limit: 60
x-ratelimit-remaining: 59
access-control-allow-origin: *
 

{
    "result": false,
    "message": "User not found",
    "user": null
}
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

POST api/v1/auth/user/login

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Body Parameters

email   string   

Must be a valid email address. Example: davis.leone@example.com

password   string   

Must be at least 6 characters. Example: V<{$k,

remember_me   boolean  optional  

Example: true

new user sign up endpoint params: first_name, last_name, email, password, password_confirmation, register_by, g-recaptcha-response

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "https://api.dev.jumpintojob.com/api/v1/auth/job-seeker/signup" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"first_name\": \"suscipit\",
    \"last_name\": \"eos\",
    \"password\": \"voluptatem\",
    \"user_type\": \"job_seeker\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "https://api.dev.jumpintojob.com/api/v1/auth/job-seeker/signup"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "first_name": "suscipit",
    "last_name": "eos",
    "password": "voluptatem",
    "user_type": "job_seeker"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (422):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
x-ratelimit-limit: 60
x-ratelimit-remaining: 58
access-control-allow-origin: *
 

{
    "message": "Password confirmation does not match",
    "errors": {
        "password": [
            "Password confirmation does not match"
        ]
    }
}
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

POST api/v1/auth/job-seeker/signup

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Body Parameters

first_name   string   

Example: suscipit

last_name   string   

Example: eos

password   string   

Example: voluptatem

user_type   string  optional  

Example: job_seeker

Must be one of:
  • job_seeker
email   string  optional  

This field is required when register_by is email.

verification_code   string  optional  
user_plan_id   string  optional  
new_email_verification_code   string  optional  
referral_code   string  optional  
g-recaptcha-response   string  optional  

new user sign up endpoint params: first_name, last_name, email, password, password_confirmation, register_by, g-recaptcha-response

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "https://api.dev.jumpintojob.com/api/v1/auth/employer/signup" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"odio\",
    \"slug\": \"iusto\",
    \"company_type\": \"deleniti\",
    \"password\": \"quasi\",
    \"user_type\": \"employer\",
    \"email\": \"brianne.ledner@example.org\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "https://api.dev.jumpintojob.com/api/v1/auth/employer/signup"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "odio",
    "slug": "iusto",
    "company_type": "deleniti",
    "password": "quasi",
    "user_type": "employer",
    "email": "brianne.ledner@example.org"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
